namespace = dg_mahayana
country_event = {
	id = dg_mahayana.001
	title = dg_mahayana.001.t
	desc = dg_mahayana.001.d
	picture = buddhist_scroll
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					culture_group = chinese_group
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = dg_mahayana.001.d_2_china
		}
		else = {
			custom_tooltip = dg_mahayana.001.d_2_others
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					culture_group = japanese
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = dg_mahayana.001.d_japan
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_mahayana.001.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				AND = {
					culture_group = japanese
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				AND = {
					culture_group = chinese_group
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				tag = IKK
			}
			OR = {
				ADM = 2
				advisor = theologian
				has_country_flag = lotus_sutra_buddhism
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 15
			modifier = {
				any_owned_province = {
					has_building = great_temple
					has_province_flag = head_temple_lotus_sutra
				}
				factor = 4
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = lotus_sutra_buddhism
				has_new_dynasty = no
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							culture_group = chinese_group
						}
						AND = {
							culture_group = japanese
						}
						culture_group = mon_khmer
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				any_owned_province = {
					has_province_modifier = temple_town_meditation
				}
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				any_owned_province = {
					has_province_modifier = temple_town_pure_land
				}
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				any_owned_province = {
					has_province_modifier = temple_town_nichiren
				}
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = lotus_sutra_buddhism
				has_country_flag = patriarch_hostile
				factor = 0.1
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = lotus_sutra_buddhism
				has_country_flag = patriarch_corrupt
				factor = 0.2
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = lotus_sutra_buddhism
				has_country_flag = patriarch_controversial
				factor = 0.5
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				government = theocracy
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = lotus_sutra_buddhism
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_ruler_modifier = {
				name = lotus_sutra_buddhism
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				religion = mahayana
				has_ruler_modifier = lotus_sutra_buddhism
				piety = 0.6
			}
			add_opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = same_doctrine_fanatical
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				religion = mahayana
				has_ruler_modifier = lotus_sutra_buddhism
				piety = 0.2
				NOT = {
					piety = 0.6
				}
			}
			add_opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = same_doctrine_pious
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				religion = mahayana
				has_ruler_modifier = lotus_sutra_buddhism
				piety = -0.2
				NOT = {
					piety = 0.2
				}
			}
			add_opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = same_doctrine_observant
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = lotus_sutra_buddhism
				piety = 0.6
			}
			add_legitimacy = 3
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = lotus_sutra_buddhism
				piety = 0.2
				NOT = {
					piety = 0.6
				}
			}
			add_legitimacy = 2
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = lotus_sutra_buddhism
				piety = -0.2
				NOT = {
					piety = 0.2
				}
			}
			add_legitimacy = 1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = meditation_buddhism
					has_country_flag = nichiren_buddhism
					has_country_flag = pure_land_buddhism
					has_country_flag = confucianism_dominates
				}
			}
			add_adm_power = -10
			clr_country_flag = meditation_buddhism
			clr_country_flag = nichiren_buddhism
			clr_country_flag = pure_land_buddhism
			clr_country_flag = clerical_advisor
			clr_country_flag = patriarch_zealous
			clr_country_flag = patriarch_theologian
			clr_country_flag = patriarch_obedient
			clr_country_flag = patriarch_controversial
			clr_country_flag = patriarch_corrupt
			clr_country_flag = patriarch_hostile
			clr_country_flag = patriarch_appointed
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = meditation_buddhism
					has_country_flag = nichiren_buddhism
					has_country_flag = pure_land_buddhism
					has_country_flag = confucianism_dominates
				}
				piety = 0.6
			}
			add_legitimacy = -3
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = meditation_buddhism
					has_country_flag = nichiren_buddhism
					has_country_flag = pure_land_buddhism
					has_country_flag = confucianism_dominates
				}
				piety = 0.2
				NOT = {
					piety = 0.6
				}
			}
			add_legitimacy = -2
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = meditation_buddhism
					has_country_flag = nichiren_buddhism
					has_country_flag = pure_land_buddhism
					has_country_flag = confucianism_dominates
				}
				piety = -0.2
				NOT = {
					piety = 0.2
				}
			}
			add_legitimacy = -1
		}
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_province_modifier = temple_town_pure_land
					has_province_modifier = temple_town_meditation
					has_province_modifier = temple_town_nichiren
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				set_variable = {
					which = added_unrest
					value = 1
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					province_event = {
						id = stacking_unrest.002
					}
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = added_unrest_1
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = pure_land_buddhism
			clr_country_flag = meditation_buddhism
			set_country_flag = lotus_sutra_buddhism
			clr_country_flag = nichiren_buddhism
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_ruler_modifier = buddhism_dominates
					religion = confucianism
				}
				every_owned_province = {
					limit = {
						religion = confucianism
						check_variable = {
							which = mahayana
							value = 2
						}
						is_core = ROOT
						culture_group = ROOT
					}
					random = {
						chance = 25
						change_variable = {
							which = mahayana
							value = 1
						}
						change_variable = {
							which = converts
							value = -1
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					culture_group = japanese
				}
				any_owned_province = {
					check_variable = {
						which = shinto
						value = 2
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = dg_shinto.001
				days = 60
			}
		}
	}
	option = {

				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_fanatical
						}
					}
					trigger_switch = {
						on_trigger = has_country_modifier
						patriarch_hostile_observant = {
							remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_observant
						}
						patriarch_hostile_pious = {
							remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_pious
						}
					}
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = patriarch_hostile_fanatical
						duration = -1
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					patriarch_authority = 0.50
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_pious
						}
					}
					trigger_switch = {
						on_trigger = has_country_modifier
						patriarch_hostile_observant = {
							remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_observant
						}
						patriarch_hostile_fanatical = {
							remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_fanatical
						}
					}
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = patriarch_hostile_pious
						duration = -1
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					patriarch_authority = 0.10
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_observant
						}
					}
					trigger_switch = {
						on_trigger = has_country_modifier
						patriarch_hostile_pious = {
							remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_pious
						}
						patriarch_hostile_fanatical = {
							remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_fanatical
						}
					}
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = patriarch_hostile_observant
						duration = -1
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				trigger_switch = {
					on_trigger = has_country_modifier
					patriarch_hostile_observant = {
						remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_observant
					}
					patriarch_hostile_pious = {
						remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_pious
					}
					patriarch_hostile_fanatical = {
						remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_fanatical
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			trigger_switch = {
				on_trigger = has_country_modifier
				patriarch_hostile_observant = {
					remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_observant
				}
				patriarch_hostile_pious = {
					remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_pious
				}
				patriarch_hostile_fanatical = {
					remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_fanatical
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

province_event = {
	id = dg_mahayana.003
	title = dg_mahayana.003.t
	desc = dg_mahayana.003.d
	picture = mahayana_prayer
	trigger = {
		has_building = great_temple
		owner = {
			religion = mahayana
		}
		owner = {
			NOT = {
				government = theocracy
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			owner = {
				has_country_flag = patriarchate_vacant
			}
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 20
		modifier = {
			NOT = {
				owner = {
					has_country_flag = patriarch_appointed
				}
			}
			factor = 0.25
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					has_country_flag = meditation_buddhism
					any_known_country = {
						AND = {
							culture_group = chinese_group
						}
						num_of_cities = 25
						AND = {
							OR = {
								is_subject = no
								is_subject_of_type = tributary_state
								is_subject_of_type = close_tributary_state
							}
						}
						NOT = {
							tag = PREV
						}
						NOT = {
							war_with = PREV
						}
						religion_group = taoic
					}
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = dg_mahayana.003.d_china
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					any_country = {
						overlord_of = ROOT
						religion_group = taoic
					}
					OR = {
						NOT = {
							has_country_flag = meditation_buddhism
						}
						NOT = {
							any_known_country = {
								AND = {
									culture_group = chinese_group
								}
								num_of_cities = 25

									OR = {
										is_subject = no

									}
								}
								NOT = {
									tag = PREV
								}
								NOT = {
									war_with = PREV
								}
								religion_group = taoic
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = dg_mahayana.003.d_vassal
		}
		owner = {
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = patriarch_hostile
					}
					set_variable = {
						which = patriarch_hostility
						value = 2
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = patriarch_controversial
					}
					set_variable = {
						which = patriarch_hostility
						value = 1
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_year = 1400
						NOT = {
							has_global_flag = abbot_rennyo
						}
						AND = {
							culture_group = japanese
						}
						any_owned_province = {
							has_province_flag = head_temple_pure_land
						}
					}
					random = {
						chance = 25
						country_event = {
							id = dg_mahayana.041
							days = 60
						}
					}
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = clerical_advisor
			clr_country_flag = patriarch_zealous
			clr_country_flag = patriarch_theologian
			clr_country_flag = patriarch_obedient
			clr_country_flag = patriarch_controversial
			clr_country_flag = patriarch_corrupt
			clr_country_flag = patriarch_hostile
			set_country_flag = patriarch_appointed
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_impotent
				}
				random = {
					chance = 60
					remove_country_modifier = unhappy_church_impotent
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_weak
				}
				random = {
					chance = 50
					remove_country_modifier = unhappy_church_weak
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_moderate
				}
				random = {
					chance = 40
					remove_country_modifier = unhappy_church_moderate
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_strong
				}
				random = {
					chance = 30
					remove_country_modifier = unhappy_church_strong
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_powerful
				}
				random = {
					chance = 20
					remove_country_modifier = unhappy_church_powerful
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_mahayana.003.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
		}
		trigger = {

				owner = {
					has_country_flag = meditation_buddhism

						}

						AND = {
							OR = {
								is_subject = no
								is_subject_of_type = tributary_state
								is_subject_of_type = close_tributary_state

				trigger_switch = {
					on_trigger = has_country_modifier
					patriarch_controversial_observant = {
						remove_country_modifier = patriarch_controversial_observant
					}
					patriarch_controversial_pious = {
						remove_country_modifier = patriarch_controversial_pious
					}
					patriarch_controversial_fanatical = {
						remove_country_modifier = patriarch_controversial_fanatical
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = patriarch_corrupt
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						patriarch_authority = 0.75
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								has_country_modifier = patriarch_corrupt_fanatical
							}
						}
						trigger_switch = {
							on_trigger = has_country_modifier
							patriarch_corrupt_observant = {
								remove_country_modifier = patriarch_corrupt_observant
							}
							patriarch_corrupt_pious = {
								remove_country_modifier = patriarch_corrupt_pious
							}
						}
						add_country_modifier = {
							name = patriarch_corrupt_fanatical
							duration = -1
						}
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						patriarch_authority = 0.50
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								has_country_modifier = patriarch_corrupt_pious
							}
						}
						trigger_switch = {
							on_trigger = has_country_modifier
							patriarch_corrupt_observant = {
								remove_country_modifier = patriarch_corrupt_observant
							}
							patriarch_corrupt_fanatical = {
								remove_country_modifier = patriarch_corrupt_fanatical
							}
						}
						add_country_modifier = {
							name = patriarch_corrupt_pious
							duration = -1
						}
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						patriarch_authority = 0.10
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								has_country_modifier = patriarch_corrupt_observant
							}
						}
						trigger_switch = {
							on_trigger = has_country_modifier
							patriarch_corrupt_pious = {
								remove_country_modifier = patriarch_corrupt_pious
							}
							patriarch_corrupt_fanatical = {
								remove_country_modifier = patriarch_corrupt_fanatical
							}
						}
						add_country_modifier = {
							name = patriarch_corrupt_observant
							duration = -1
						}
					}
				}
				else = {
					trigger_switch = {
						on_trigger = has_country_modifier
						patriarch_corrupt_observant = {
							remove_country_modifier = patriarch_corrupt_observant
						}
						patriarch_corrupt_pious = {
							remove_country_modifier = patriarch_corrupt_pious
						}
						patriarch_corrupt_fanatical = {
							remove_country_modifier = patriarch_corrupt_fanatical
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				trigger_switch = {
					on_trigger = has_country_modifier
					patriarch_corrupt_observant = {
						remove_country_modifier = patriarch_corrupt_observant
					}
					patriarch_corrupt_pious = {
						remove_country_modifier = patriarch_corrupt_pious
					}
					patriarch_corrupt_fanatical = {
						remove_country_modifier = patriarch_corrupt_fanatical
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = patriarch_hostile
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						patriarch_authority = 0.75
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								has_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_fanatical
							}
						}
						trigger_switch = {
							on_trigger = has_country_modifier
							patriarch_hostile_observant = {
								remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_observant
							}
							patriarch_hostile_pious = {
								remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_pious
							}
						}
						add_country_modifier = {
							name = patriarch_hostile_fanatical
							duration = -1
						}
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						patriarch_authority = 0.50
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								has_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_pious
							}
						}
						trigger_switch = {
							on_trigger = has_country_modifier
							patriarch_hostile_observant = {
								remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_observant
							}
							patriarch_hostile_fanatical = {
								remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_fanatical
							}
						}
						add_country_modifier = {
							name = patriarch_hostile_pious
							duration = -1
						}
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						patriarch_authority = 0.10
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								has_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_observant
							}
						}
						trigger_switch = {
							on_trigger = has_country_modifier
							patriarch_hostile_pious = {
								remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_pious
							}
							patriarch_hostile_fanatical = {
								remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_fanatical
							}
						}
						add_country_modifier = {
							name = patriarch_hostile_observant
							duration = -1
						}
					}
				}
				else = {
					trigger_switch = {
						on_trigger = has_country_modifier
						patriarch_hostile_observant = {
							remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_observant
						}
						patriarch_hostile_pious = {
							remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_pious
						}
						patriarch_hostile_fanatical = {
							remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_fanatical
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				trigger_switch = {
					on_trigger = has_country_modifier
					patriarch_hostile_observant = {
						remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_observant
					}
					patriarch_hostile_pious = {
						remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_pious
					}
					patriarch_hostile_fanatical = {
						remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_fanatical
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
province_event = {
	id = dg_mahayana.006
	title = dg_mahayana.006.t
	desc = dg_mahayana.006.d
	picture = mahayana_temple_destroyed
	trigger = {
		has_province_modifier = feuding_monks
		had_province_flag = {
			flag = monks_feuding
			days = 120
		}
		has_province_flag = feud_pure_land
		NOT = {
			has_province_flag = feud_1_pure_land
		}
		NOT = {
			has_province_flag = feud_2_pure_land
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 25
		modifier = {
			has_province_flag = ikki_league
			factor = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			OR = {
				has_province_flag = feud_2_lotus_sutra
				has_province_flag = feud_2_nichiren
				has_province_flag = feud_2_meditation
			}
			factor = 0.3
		}
		modifier = {
			OR = {
				has_province_flag = feud_1_lotus_sutra
				has_province_flag = feud_1_nichiren
				has_province_flag = feud_1_meditation
			}
			factor = 0.6
		}
		modifier = {
			has_province_flag = feud_stalemate
			factor = 2
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_flag = feud_lotus_sutra
			}
			custom_tooltip = lotus_sutra_wins
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_flag = feud_nichiren
			}
			custom_tooltip = nichiren_wins
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_flag = feud_meditation
			}
			custom_tooltip = meditation_wins
		}
		remove_province_modifier = temple_town_pure_land
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_flag = head_temple_pure_land
				has_province_flag = head_temple_pure_land_weakened
			}
			clr_province_flag = head_temple_pure_land
			clr_province_flag = head_temple_pure_land_weakened
			custom_tooltip = lost_head_temple
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_flag = head_temple_pure_land
				NOT = {
					has_province_flag = head_temple_pure_land_weakened
				}
			}
			set_province_flag = head_temple_pure_land_weakened
			custom_tooltip = bribed_head_temple
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_province_flag = monks_feuding
			clr_province_flag = feud_pure_land
			clr_province_flag = feud_lotus_sutra
			clr_province_flag = feud_nichiren
			clr_province_flag = feud_meditation
			clr_province_flag = feud_stalemate
			clr_province_flag = feud_1_pure_land
			clr_province_flag = feud_1_lotus_sutra
			clr_province_flag = feud_1_nichiren
			clr_province_flag = feud_1_meditation
			clr_province_flag = feud_2_pure_land
			clr_province_flag = feud_2_lotus_sutra
			clr_province_flag = feud_2_nichiren
			clr_province_flag = feud_2_meditation
			set_variable = {
				which = strength_pure_land
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = strength_lotus_sutra
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = strength_nichiren
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = strength_meditation
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = daimyo_strength
				value = 0
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_mahayana.006.a
		remove_province_modifier = feuding_monks
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = ikki_league
			}
			remove_province_modifier = ikki_league
			hidden_effect = {
				IKK = {
					change_variable = {
						which = ikko_threat
						value = -1
					}
				}
			}
		}
		owner = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = pure_land_buddhism
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						piety = 0.60
					}
					add_prestige = -2
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						piety = 0.20
					}
					add_prestige = -1.5
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						piety = -0.20
					}
					add_prestige = -1
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						piety = -0.60
					}
					add_prestige = -0.5
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = dg_mahayana.007

		}

			}

				}

						change_variable = {

							value = 1
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

			clr_province_flag = head_temple_lotus_sutra_weakened
			custom_tooltip = lost_head_temple
		}
		if = {

				has_province_flag = head_temple_lotus_sutra
				NOT = {
					has_province_flag = head_temple_lotus_sutra_weakened
				}
			}
			set_province_flag = head_temple_lotus_sutra_weakened
			custom_tooltip = bribed_head_temple
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_province_flag = monks_feuding
			clr_province_flag = feud_pure_land
			clr_province_flag = feud_lotus_sutra
			clr_province_flag = feud_nichiren
			clr_province_flag = feud_meditation
			clr_province_flag = feud_stalemate
			clr_province_flag = feud_1_pure_land
			clr_province_flag = feud_1_lotus_sutra
			clr_province_flag = feud_1_nichiren
			clr_province_flag = feud_1_meditation
			clr_province_flag = feud_2_pure_land
			clr_province_flag = feud_2_lotus_sutra
			clr_province_flag = feud_2_nichiren
			clr_province_flag = feud_2_meditation
			set_variable = {
				which = strength_pure_land
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = strength_lotus_sutra
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = strength_nichiren
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = strength_meditation
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = daimyo_strength
				value = 0
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_mahayana.006.a
		remove_province_modifier = feuding_monks
		owner = {
			if = {

					}

			custom_tooltip = lotus_sutra_wins
		}

						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		remove_province_modifier = temple_town_meditation
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_flag = head_temple_meditation
				has_province_flag = head_temple_meditation_weakened
			}
			clr_province_flag = head_temple_meditation
			clr_province_flag = head_temple_meditation_weakened
			custom_tooltip = lost_head_temple
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_flag = head_temple_meditation
				NOT = {
					has_province_flag = head_temple_meditation_weakened
				}
			}
			set_province_flag = head_temple_meditation_weakened
			custom_tooltip = bribed_head_temple
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_province_flag = monks_feuding
			clr_province_flag = feud_pure_land
			clr_province_flag = feud_lotus_sutra
			clr_province_flag = feud_nichiren
			clr_province_flag = feud_meditation
			clr_province_flag = feud_stalemate
			clr_province_flag = feud_1_pure_land
			clr_province_flag = feud_1_lotus_sutra
			clr_province_flag = feud_1_nichiren
			clr_province_flag = feud_1_meditation
			clr_province_flag = feud_2_pure_land
			clr_province_flag = feud_2_lotus_sutra
			clr_province_flag = feud_2_nichiren
			clr_province_flag = feud_2_meditation
			set_variable = {
				which = strength_pure_land
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = strength_lotus_sutra
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = strength_nichiren
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = strength_meditation
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = daimyo_strength
				value = 0
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_mahayana.006.a
		remove_province_modifier = feuding_monks
		owner = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = meditation_buddhism
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						piety = 0.60
					}
					add_prestige = -2
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						piety = 0.20
					}
					add_prestige = -1.5
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						piety = -0.20
					}
					add_prestige = -1
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						piety = -0.60
					}
					add_prestige = -0.5
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

			}
			factor = 0.5
		}

			factor = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			has_province_modifier = temple_town_nichiren
			factor = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			has_province_modifier = temple_town_meditation
			factor = 2
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_mahayana.010.a

			factor = 80
		}
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = temple_town_pure_land
			duration = -1

			}

					id = stacking_unrest.002
				}
			}
		}

	desc = dg_mahayana.010.d
	picture = mahayana_temple
	trigger = {
		religion = mahayana
		OR = {
			has_province_flag = head_temple_meditation
			any_neighbor_province = {
				has_province_flag = head_temple_meditation
			}
			any_neighbor_province = {
				any_neighbor_province = {
					has_province_flag = head_temple_meditation
				}
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			has_province_modifier = temple_town_meditation
		}
		owner = {
			OR = {
				religion = mahayana
				AND = {
					has_country_modifier = buddhism_dominates
					religion_group = taoic
				}
			}
			patriarch_authority = 0.50
			OR = {
				NOT = {
					ADM = 2
				}
				piety = 0.60
				AND = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_modifier = lotus_sutra_buddhism
					}
					NOT = {
						has_country_modifier = pure_land_buddhism
					}
					NOT = {
						has_country_modifier = nichiren_buddhism
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 20
		modifier = {
			owner = {
				has_country_modifier = meditation_buddhism
			}
			factor = 0.5
		}
		modifier = {
			has_province_flag = head_temple_meditation
			factor = 0.5
		}
		modifier = {
			NOT = {
				has_province_flag = head_temple_meditation
			}
			NOT = {

					has_province_flag = head_temple_meditation

				patriarch_authority = 0.75
			}
			factor = 0.5
		}
		modifier = {
			has_province_modifier = temple_town_lotus_sutra
			factor = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			has_province_modifier = temple_town_nichiren
			factor = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			has_province_modifier = temple_town_pure_land
			factor = 2
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_mahayana.010.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
		}
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = temple_town_meditation
			duration = -1
		}

			set_variable = {
				which = added_unrest
				value = -2
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				province_event = {
					id = stacking_unrest.002
				}
			}
		}

	}

		name = dg_mahayana.010.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				owner = {

				}

			}

			}

				factor = 1.4
			}

			}
			modifier = {

				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				has_province_modifier = temple_town_nichiren
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = {
					ADM = 6
				}
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = {
					ADM = 5
				}
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					owner = {
						ADM = 3
					}
				}
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					owner = {
						ADM = 4
					}
				}
				factor = 0.7
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				owner = {
					has_country_modifier = meditation_buddhism
				}
			}
			owner = {
				ADM = 2
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = {
				which = added_unrest
				value = 2
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				province_event = {
					id = stacking_unrest.002
				}
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = added_unrest_2
		owner = {
			add_adm_power = -5
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_province_modifier = temple_town_meditation
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					set_variable = {
						which = added_unrest
						value = 1
					}
					hidden_effect = {
						province_event = {
							id = stacking_unrest.002
						}
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = added_unrest_1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					ADM = 5
					NOT = {
						ADM = 6
					}
				}
			}
			random = {
				chance = 10
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = temple_town_meditation
					duration = -1
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					ADM = 4
				}
			}
			random = {
				chance = 30
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = temple_town_meditation
					duration = -1
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					ADM = 3
				}
			}
			random = {
				chance = 50
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = temple_town_meditation
					duration = -1
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					ADM = 2
				}
			}
			random = {
				chance = 70
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = temple_town_meditation
					duration = -1
				}
			}
		}
	}

country_event = {
	id = dg_mahayana.042
	title = dg_mahayana.042.t
	desc = dg_mahayana.042.d
	picture = mahayana_prayer
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = dg_mahayana.042.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = pure_land_buddhism
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					piety = 0.60
				}
				add_prestige = 2
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = 0.20
				}
				add_prestige = 1.5
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = -0.20
				}
				add_prestige = 1
			}
			else = {
				add_prestige = 0.5
			}
		}
	}
}
province_event = {
	id = dg_mahayana.043
	title = dg_mahayana.043.t
	desc = dg_mahayana.043.d
	picture = mahayana_temple
	trigger = {
		AND = {
			culture_group = japanese
		}
		has_global_flag = abbot_rennyo
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = ikko_ikki
		}
		religion = mahayana
		OR = {
			has_province_flag = head_temple_pure_land
			any_neighbor_province = {
				has_province_flag = head_temple_pure_land
			}
			any_neighbor_province = {
				any_neighbor_province = {
					has_province_flag = head_temple_pure_land
				}
			}
			owner = {
				has_country_modifier = pure_land_buddhism
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			has_province_modifier = temple_town_pure_land
		}
		owner = {
			OR = {
				religion = mahayana
				AND = {
					has_country_modifier = buddhism_dominates
					religion_group = taoic
				}
			}
			patriarch_authority = 0.40
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 20
		modifier = {
			owner = {
				has_country_modifier = pure_land_buddhism
			}
			factor = 0.5
		}
		modifier = {
			has_province_flag = head_temple_pure_land
			factor = 0.5
		}
		modifier = {
			NOT = {
				has_province_flag = head_temple_pure_land
			}
			NOT = {
				any_neighbor_province = {
					has_province_flag = head_temple_pure_land
				}
			}
			factor = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = {
				patriarch_authority = 0.75
			}
			factor = 0.5
		}
		modifier = {
			has_province_modifier = temple_town_lotus_sutra
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			has_province_modifier = temple_town_nichiren
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			has_province_modifier = temple_town_meditation
			factor = 1.4
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_mahayana.043.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
		}
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = temple_town_pure_land
			duration = -1
		}
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = monastic_town
			duration = 5000
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = {
				which = added_unrest
				value = -2
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				province_event = {
					id = stacking_unrest.002
				}
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = added_unrest_2
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_mahayana.043.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				owner = {
					has_country_modifier = meditation_buddhism
				}
				factor = 1.4

							}
							patriarch_hostile_pious = {
								remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_pious
							}
						}
						add_country_modifier = {
							name = patriarch_hostile_fanatical
							duration = -1
						}
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						patriarch_authority = 0.50
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								has_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_pious
							}
						}
						trigger_switch = {
							on_trigger = has_country_modifier
							patriarch_hostile_observant = {
								remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_observant
							}
							patriarch_hostile_fanatical = {
								remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_fanatical
							}
						}
						add_country_modifier = {
							name = patriarch_hostile_pious
							duration = -1
						}
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						patriarch_authority = 0.10
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								has_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_observant
							}
						}
						trigger_switch = {
							on_trigger = has_country_modifier
							patriarch_hostile_pious = {
								remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_pious
							}
							patriarch_hostile_fanatical = {
								remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_fanatical
							}
						}
						add_country_modifier = {
							name = patriarch_hostile_observant
							duration = -1
						}
					}
				}
				else = {
					trigger_switch = {
						on_trigger = has_country_modifier
						patriarch_hostile_observant = {
							remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_observant
						}
						patriarch_hostile_pious = {
							remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_pious
						}
						patriarch_hostile_fanatical = {
							remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_fanatical
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				trigger_switch = {
					on_trigger = has_country_modifier
					patriarch_hostile_observant = {
						remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_observant
					}
					patriarch_hostile_pious = {
						remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_pious
					}
					patriarch_hostile_fanatical = {
						remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_fanatical
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

							which = daimyo_strength
							value = 6
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_province_flag = feud_2_meditation
					}
					clr_province_flag = feud_2_meditation
					set_province_flag = feud_1_meditation
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_province_flag = feud_2_lotus_sutra
					}
					clr_province_flag = feud_2_lotus_sutra
					set_province_flag = feud_1_lotus_sutra
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_province_flag = feud_2_nichiren
					}
					clr_province_flag = feud_2_nichiren
					set_province_flag = feud_1_nichiren
				}
			}
		}
		owner = {
			add_mil_power = -10
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = {
				which = strength_pure_land
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = strength_lotus_sutra
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = strength_nichiren
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = strength_meditation
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = daimyo_strength
				value = 0
			}
		}
	}
}

province_event = {
	id = dg_mahayana.053
	title = dg_mahayana.053.t
	desc = dg_mahayana.053.d
	picture = mahayana_sohei
	trigger = {
		owned_by = IKK
		NOT = {
			has_province_modifier = ikki_league
		}
		AND = {
			culture_group = japanese
		}
		religion = mahayana
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 1
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_mahayana.053.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_global_flag = ikko_ikki
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = ikko_ikki
		}
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = ikki_league
			duration = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = ikko_ikki
					}
				}
			}
			owner = {
				set_country_flag = ikko_ikki
				add_ruler_modifier = {
					name = sword_of_faith
				}
			}
		}
		owner = {
			add_yearly_manpower = 0.05
			every_known_country = {
				limit = {
					religion = mahayana
					AND = {
						culture_group = japanese
					}
					NOT = {
						government = theocracy
					}
					OR = {
						is_neighbor_of = PREV
						war_with = PREV
						has_country_flag = ikko_ikki_rebels
						has_country_flag = pure_land_banned
					}
				}
				add_opinion = {
					who = PREV
					modifier = supporting_religious_rebels
				}
				add_casus_belli = {
					target = PREV
					type = cb_annex
					months = 50
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = dg_mahayana.055
	title = dg_mahayana.055.t
	desc = dg_mahayana.055.d
	picture = buddhist_scroll
	trigger = {
		religion = mahayana
		has_global_flag = ikko_ikki

			religious_unity = 1.00
		}
		num_of_cities = 15
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = 1615_decree
		}
		is_at_war = no
		NOT = {
			any_owned_province = {
				has_province_modifier = ikki_league
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			has_spawned_rebels = ikko_ikki_rebels
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 20
	}
	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = 1615_decree
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_mahayana.055.a
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				culture_group = japanese
			}
			any_owned_province = {
				check_variable = {
					which = shinto
					value = 2
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
		}
		custom_tooltip = convert_10
		custom_tooltip = shinto_10
		custom_tooltip = confucianism_10
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_province = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_owner_religion = yes
					}
					random_list = {
						50 = {
							hidden_effect = {
								change_variable = {
									which = shinto
									value = 2
								}
								change_variable = {
									which = province_religion
									value = 2
								}
							}
						}
						50 = {
							hidden_effect = {
								change_variable = {
									which = confucianism
									value = 2
								}
								change_variable = {
									which = province_religion
									value = 2
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				else = {
					hidden_effect = {
						change_variable = {
							which = converted_heathens
							value = 2
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_mahayana.055.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = religious_tolerance
			}
			remove_country_modifier = religious_tolerance
			add_piety = 0.40
		}
		else = {
			add_piety = 0.20
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = religious_intolerance
			duration = 5000
		}
		custom_tooltip = convert_10
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_owner_religion = yes
					}
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					change_variable = {
						which = converted_heathens
						value = 2
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_mahayana.055.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		set_country_flag = shared_moral_authority
		add_patriarch_authority = -0.10
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = religious_intolerance
			}
			remove_country_modifier = religious_intolerance
			add_piety = -0.40
		}
		else = {
			add_piety = -0.20
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = religious_tolerance
			duration = 5000
		}
	}
